  <script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
        var contextPath = '/jira';
        var eventBuffer = [];

        function printDeprecatedMsg() {
            if (console && console.warn) {
                console.warn('DEPRECATED JS - contextPath global variable has been deprecated since 7.4.0. Use `wrm/context-path` module instead.');
            }
        }

        function sendEvent(analytics, postfix) {
            analytics.send({
                name: 'js.globals.contextPath.' + postfix
            });
        }

        function sendDeprecatedEvent(postfix) {
            try {
                var analytics = require('jira/analytics');
                if (eventBuffer.length) {
                    eventBuffer.forEach(function(value) {
                        sendEvent(analytics, value);
                    });
                    eventBuffer = [];
                }

                if (postfix) {
                    sendEvent(analytics, postfix);
                }
            } catch(ex) {
                eventBuffer.push(postfix);
                setTimeout(sendDeprecatedEvent, 1000);
            }
        }

        Object.defineProperty(window, 'contextPath', {
            get: function() {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('get');
                return contextPath;
            },
            set: function(value) {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('set');
                contextPath = value;
            }
        });
    })();

</script>

                <h2 class="toggle-title">Description</h2>
               </div>
               <div class="mod-content">
                <div id="description-val" class="field-ignore-highlight"> 
                 <div class="user-content-block"> 
                  <p>Multiple errors during teardown while trying to delete files/directories of the test databases on vista against sun jdk16 on vista, but passed against same jvm on sun nightly runs againstlinux and solaris.</p> 
                  <p>As of time of this report the tests against other sun jvms had not finished. Errors were also seen in ibm nightly runs, I'll rerport those in following comments.</p> 
                  <p>The following checkin that was included in the reported test failures changed the Native authentication tests, so seems likely to have caused the issues:<br> r1233377 | rhillegas | 2012-01-19 14:51:13 +0100 (Thu, 19 Jan 2012) | 1 line<br> First version of NATIVE authentication service, including first tranche of tests for it.</p> 
                  <p>vista run had 6 errors:<br> <a href="http://dbtg.foundry.sun.com/derby/test/Daily/jvm1.6/testing/testlog/vista/1233467-suitesAll_diff.txt" class="external-link" rel="nofollow">http://dbtg.foundry.sun.com/derby/test/Daily/jvm1.6/testing/testlog/vista/1233467-suitesAll_diff.txt</a><br> 1) testAll(org.apache.derbyTesting.functionTests.tests.lang.NativeAuthenticationServiceTest)junit.framework.AssertionFailedError: Failed to delete 77 files (root=C:\cludev\jagtmp\autoderbyN_regression\suitesAll_7\log\system\singleUse\oneuse1d): C:\cludev\jagtmp\autoderbyN_regression\suitesAll_7\log\system\singleUse\oneuse1d\db.lck (isDir=false, canRead=true, canWrite=true, size=38), C:\cludev\jagtmp\autoderbyN_regression\suitesAll_7\log\system\singleUse\oneuse1d\log\log1.dat (isDir=false, canRead=true, canWrite=true, size=1048576), \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003ethe main difference on windows with other OS\'s that I have seen is that you can\'t delete files that another process has open. Hopefully some others\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\ncan comment on specific junit fixes that have helped in the past.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eCould you describe at high level what one of the test fixtures that is failing is doing. The tests create a lot of single-use databases, which are deleted between test runs. The tests also shut down the engine. The order of cleanup steps should be:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e1) Bring down the engine.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e2) Delete the database directories without explicitly shutting down the databases.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe tests behave like this because one of the databases, the credentials database, is needed in order to authenticate the request to shutdown the engine. The credentials database has to still exist when the request to shutdown the engine is processed. The engine needs to be down before the next test runs so that the next test will create its own system-wide authentication service.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eIs the directory deletion blocked by open file handles?
